Important News

Zhang Qun Discusses the Current Situation in Beiping

The Central Government Will Take Effective Sanctions Against Guangdong if Necessary

Beiping Correspondence: Shanghai Mayor Zhang Qun, under the orders of Chairman Jiang, came to Beiping to celebrate Vice Commander Zhang's birthday. He arrived in Beiping at noon today (the 3rd) and stayed at the Beiping Hotel. Reporters went to visit him and were received by Mr. Zhang in the downstairs living room. He spoke at length about various issues regarding the current situation. The following is a record of his conversation:

Mission to the North: This time, I, as a brother, came to Beiping under the orders of Chairman Jiang to celebrate Vice Commander Zhang's birthday. When leaving Nanjing, Chairman Jiang also received news that Vice Commander Zhang was ill, so he instructed me to inquire about his condition in the North. It was only when I saw the newspaper in Tianjin this morning that I learned that the Vice Commander had been admitted to the hospital for recuperation. I suspect that the Vice Commander fell ill during his visit to Nanjing to attend the National Convention, due to the poor weather in the South and the constant rain, or perhaps he caught a cold and was exhausted from the journey. However, this kind of common illness can be cured with a little rest. My purpose here is solely to celebrate the birthday and inquire about the illness, nothing else. It has not yet been decided when I will visit the Vice Commander.

The Course of Events in Guangdong: In the ten days before the opening of the National Convention, various rumors circulated in Nanjing, saying that the Guangdong side was preparing to take unfavorable actions against the Central Government at the opening of the convention. At the same time, Chen Mingshu, Chairman of Guangdong Province, also sent a telegram reporting that he was being forced to go to Hong Kong. At that time, the Central Government believed that the sacrifices made to quell the rebellions in the past had been great, and that the goal of peace and unification had just been achieved. Moreover, the people of the whole country were eagerly hoping for peace and unification, and no one would want to come out again to undermine it. Therefore, it was believed that the rumors were absolutely unfounded. It was not until April 30 that telegrams were received from Gu Yingfen, Chen Jitang, and others that the Central Government began to believe that the rumors were true. As a revolutionary soldier, Chen Jitang should have taken obedience as his duty and should not have interfered rashly. After receiving this telegram, the Central Government still believed that it was a misunderstanding and instructed the Supervisory Committee to send a telegram to explain everything, hoping to clarify the situation. Most of the telegrams exchanged have been published in newspapers everywhere, so I think you can read them. According to the Guangdong side, they hoped that a sudden blow before the opening of the National Convention could prevent representatives from all over the country from entering Nanjing to attend the convention, thus preventing the convention from being held. Who knew that in fact, it had the opposite effect, and the representatives from all over the country became even more united. All the representatives, except for Guangxi, which had special circumstances and could not participate in time, attended completely. However, the Guangdong incident had a slight impact on foreign affairs. Originally, the Central Government had decided to completely abolish all unequal treaties and consular jurisdiction before the opening of the National Convention, but this matter was temporarily suspended due to this incident. However, the internal affairs of Guangdong are indeed very complicated, and they are not harmonious with each other at all. Take Gu Yingfen and Sun Ke as an example. Previously, at a meeting of the State Council, they had a major dispute over the issue of opening Zhongshan Port, almost to the point of using force. It was only after Chairman Jiang mediated that the matter was settled. Moreover, now Guangdong wants to merge all factions into one furnace. I wonder if they can truly trust each other. Just like the Beiping Enlarged Conference last year, many jokes were made. You can see a glimpse of the current situation by examining the events of the past. Moreover, the current makeshift coalition in Guangdong is not even as good as the assembly at the Enlarged Conference last year. I believe they don't have much ability. To put it bluntly, they are just making trouble.

The Central Government's Attitude: As for the Central Government, it still adheres to a peaceful solution as of now, hoping that they can come to their senses and avoid causing suffering to the people. If they are determined not to repent and are willing to undermine peace, then the Central Government will have no choice but to take necessary and effective sanctions. In short, the Central Government is waiting for their final awakening regarding the Guangdong issue.

Mediation Efforts: In addition, Mr. Zhang Puquan went to Guangdong a few days ago to mediate, which was also to convey the Central Government's intention to respect peace. Moreover, Mr. Zhang is a person who deeply loves peace and hopes that this matter will not escalate, so he personally went there despite his fatigue. However, because the elements in Guangdong are complicated and no one is responsible, I am afraid that a satisfactory result cannot be obtained. Although Mr. Zhang knows that it is useless, he will still go in the hope of a miracle, because all the comrades in the Central Government have adhered to the premise of a peaceful solution from beginning to end. Now I hear that Mr. Zhang will return to Nanjing to report in the next few days.

Recent Situation of Hu and Li: The Guangdong side has picked up rumors and made a fuss, claiming that Mr. Hu Hanmin's actions in Nanjing are not free. This is greatly inconsistent with the facts. After resigning, Mr. Hu rested at home due to physical discomfort. A few days ago, he even sent a telegram to Guangdong, advising them to cherish the Party and the country and to pay attention to peace. His actions are very free. Not only can comrades from the Central Government visit him, but also representatives who attended the National Convention visited him several times a few days ago, and they chatted casually without any restrictions. Mr. Hu has a deep reputation in the Party and the country. Although his words and deeds and his opinions may be unique, they are Mr. Hu's own insights. This is a common thing. Hu does not want to be surrounded by all parties, so he is unwilling to go elsewhere at this time, fearing that it will damage his revolutionary history. In fact, even if Hu wants to go elsewhere, the Central Government will let him go and will not interfere in the slightest. How can it be said that his actions are not free? Secondly, Mr. Li Jishen has already moved to a private residence to recuperate and is not subject to any restrictions.

剿匪 Question: The Central Government's bandit suppression is not affected in any way and will continue to advance according to the original plan. The army is now gathered in Jiangxi Province for a thorough suppression and will not be abandoned due to the Guangdong incident. The recent deployment of a large army is aimed at clearing up this matter in the short term, so this is not a concern.

Whereabouts of Wang and Wu: President Wang Chonghui is still in Shanghai and will soon leave for The Hague to attend the International Court of Justice conference. Before leaving, he plans to go to Nanjing once. As for Mr. Wu Tiecheng, he travels back and forth between Nanjing and Shanghai on official business. When I left Nanjing, he was still in Shanghai, and he may have returned to Nanjing by now. Finally, Zhang said that he originally planned to stay for a few days and then return to Nanjing. Now, because the Vice Commander is recuperating in the hospital, he must wait until he meets him to convey Chairman Jiang's birthday wishes and greetings before deciding on the date of departure from Beiping. He also plans to exchange views with Mayor Hu and others on the issue of Beiping's prosperity. As for the opening date of the Central Plenary Session, it has not yet been decided and will be decided after discussion by the Central Standing Committee. (Central News Agency)

145th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan

Resolved that There is No Need to Draft a Separate Law for Qianzhuang (Native Banks)

Revised and Approved the Draft Business Tax Law

The Legislative Yuan held its 145th meeting at 8:00 am on the 6th. 28 members including Liu Linxun attended. Chairman Shao Yuanchong discussed the following matters: (1) Review of the draft Ship Load Line Law. Resolved to submit it to the Commercial Law Drafting Committee for review. (2) Report from the Commercial Law Drafting Committee of this Yuan on the interpretation of whether state-owned and state-private joint ventures can join the Chamber of Commerce. Resolved to approve the review report. State-private joint ventures can join the Chamber of Commerce, but state-owned ones do not need to. (3) Report from the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of the management methods for Lama temples in various Mongol banners and Qinghai, the registration regulations for Mongolian Lama temples, and the resolution on various religious cases of the Mongolian Conference. Resolved that the amendment to the Mongolian Lama Temple Supervision Regulations be approved. (4) Review and amendment of the draft articles of the Xiangshi Law. Resolved that the amended articles of the Xiangshi Law be approved as amended. (5) Report from the Commercial Law Drafting Committee of this Yuan on the review of the case submitted by the Shanghai Qianye Guild (Native Bank Association) and others requesting the drafting of a separate Qianzhuang Law. Resolved to approve the review report that there is no need to draft a separate Qianzhuang Law. (6) Report from the Finance Committee of this Yuan jointly with the Economic Committee on drafting the draft Business Tax Law. Resolved to approve it with amendments.

Legislative Yuan Passes the Full Text of the Business Tax Law

The Legislative Yuan passed the full text of the Business Tax Law as amended at its 145th meeting on the 6th:

(Article 1) Business tax is a local revenue. All businesses operating in the provinces and cities directly under the Executive Yuan, except for factories that pay production tax to the central government or banks organized as joint-stock companies that pay income tax, shall pay business tax. The term "business" in the preceding paragraph refers to all enterprises for profit, but agriculture is not included. (Article 2) The income from tobacco and alcohol license taxes collected by the central government, after deducting one-tenth for the central government, shall be allocated to the respective provinces and cities as local revenue. (Article 3) All businesses subject to business tax shall apply for a business tax investigation certificate, stating the following items: (1) Type of business, name and location of the store; (2) Name, origin and address of the business operator; (3) Amount of business capital; (4) Total annual business income; (5) Total annual net business income. The business tax investigation certificate in the preceding paragraph shall be renewed annually free of charge and without levying any taxes or fees. (Article 4) The business tax rate shall be determined by the provincial or municipal governments according to the nature and condition of local businesses, based on the following three tax standards: A. If the standard is the total business income, the tax rate shall be 2 to 10 per mille of the total business income. B. If the standard is the amount of business capital, the tax rate shall be 4 to 20 per mille of the amount of business capital. C. If the standard is the net business income, the tax rate shall be as follows: (1) For net income less than 15% of the capital, the tax rate shall be 2% to less than 5% of the net income; (2) For net income equal to 15% to less than 25% of the capital, the tax rate shall be 5% to less than 7.5% of the net income; (3) For net income equal to or greater than 25% of the capital, the tax rate shall be 7.5% to 10% of the net income. (Article 5) When the total business income is used as the tax base for business tax, those with a total annual business income of less than 1,000 yuan shall be exempt from tax; when the amount of business capital is used as the tax base, those with a business capital of less than 500 yuan shall be exempt from tax; when the net business income is used as the tax base, those with a net business income of less than 100 yuan shall be exempt from tax. (Article 6) Public businesses run by the central government and local governments are exempt from business tax, but state-private joint ventures are not included. Cooperatives and factories for the poor that do not operate for profit may be exempt from business tax. (Article 7) Business tax may be levied annually, semi-annually, or by commissioned collection, which shall be determined by the provincial or municipal governments according to the circumstances. However, short-term businesses may be levied monthly according to the provisions of Articles 3 to 6. (Article 8) No surtax shall be levied on business tax. (Article 9) Business tax shall be paid directly by the taxpayer to the collecting agency and shall not be contracted out or handled by others. (Article 10) The original tooth tax, pawnbroker tax, slaughter tax and other business taxes in each province and city that should be banned or implicitly prohibited by law may be temporarily changed to business tax according to the original tax rates. (Article 11) If the financial authorities of each province or city deem that the amount stated by the business operator in accordance with Articles 3, Paragraph 1, Items 3 to 5 is inaccurate, they may establish a business tax review committee for assessment. The organization of the aforementioned review committee shall be determined by the provincial or municipal governments themselves, but the review committee members representing the interests of taxpayers shall not be less than one-third of the total number of members. (Article 12) The financial authorities of each province and city shall announce the collected business tax on a regular basis and prepare a report form to be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for verification. The Ministry of Finance and the Audit Department may send personnel to inspect or audit the collection of business tax in each province and city. (Article 13) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Fifth Division Commander Hu Zuyu Dies of Injuries

The Battle of Guangchang

Hu Dies After Being Shot Multiple Times

The Funeral Will Be Held on the 4th

Nanchang Correspondence: Fifth Division Commander Hu Zuyu led his troops into Jiangxi last year to encircle and suppress the bandits and communists. He fought from northern Jiangxi to Yiheng, Yihuang, and Nanfeng, traversing thousands of miles and repeatedly capturing famous cities. This time, Zhu Mao fled from Donggu to Ji'an, but failed. Then, they turned to attack Nanfeng and Guangchang. On May 27, Commander Hu personally led a part of the Fifth Division in a fierce battle with the bandit troops of Huang Gonglue and Hu Zhusheng in the vicinity of Guangchang County. Commander Hu took the lead, but as the red bandits became more and more numerous and lost contact before and after, he was surrounded by bandits. Commander Hu charged left and right and was shot by multiple bullets, but he refused to retreat. He was rescued from the encirclement by his orderly under the cover of night and rushed to Nanchang Hospital for treatment. However, due to his serious injuries, he died in Nanchang Hospital on the 3rd of this month. All officers and soldiers of the division and the citizens of Nanchang mourned him. Director He was especially saddened and has telegraphed the central government requesting commendation. The Fifth Division Headquarters issued a notice yesterday, stating that the funeral will be held at the Zhongshan Memorial Hall on the 4th: "Commander Hu Gongzhuo of the Fifth Division engaged in a fierce battle with the red bandits in the Guangchang campaign on May 27. He personally led the front line and fought bravely. He was seriously injured and died in Nanchang Hospital at You Shi (5-7 pm) on the 3rd of this month after ineffective treatment. The remains will be moved to the Zhongshan Memorial Hall that evening, and the funeral will be held at Shen Shi (3-5 pm) on the 4th. This is to inform you." (June 4)

Wei Lihuang's Troops Reorganized as the 10th Division

Bengbu Correspondence: After the 10th Division of the Army was reduced to a brigade, the number of the 10th Division was effectively abolished. Recently, Commander-in-Chief Jiang, considering the necessity of restoring the name of the 10th Division, specially ordered the 45th Division of the Army to be reorganized as the 10th Division of the Army and appointed Wei Lihuang, the commander of the 45th Division, as the commander of the 10th Division. The 265th Regiment, commanded by Fu Yikun, was renamed the 55th Regiment. The 266th Regiment, commanded by Wang Renqu, was renamed the 56th Regiment. The 267th Regiment, commanded by Xu Dunrong, was renamed the 57th Regiment. (2) The 135th Brigade, commanded by Li Shusen, was renamed the 30th Brigade. The 268th Regiment, commanded by Long Qiwu, was renamed the 58th Regiment. The 269th Regiment, commanded by Jiang Ji, was renamed the 59th Regiment. The 270th Regiment, commanded by Liu Zixin, was renamed the 60th Regiment. (3) The Independent Brigade, commanded by Chen Buyun, was renamed the Independent Brigade of the 10th Division. The 1st Regiment, commanded by Mei E, the 2nd Regiment, commanded by Li Xian, and the 3rd Regiment, commanded by Du Zhicheng, all under the jurisdiction of the Chen Brigade, were renamed the 1st Regiment, 2nd Regiment, and 3rd Regiment of the Independent Brigade of the 10th Division. Preliminary Survey Work for Guiding the Huai River

Establishing Water Level, Flow Rate, and Rainfall Stations

Zhuang Songnan and Others Set Off for Surveying

Bengbu Correspondence: The Guiding the Huai River Committee has formulated a concrete plan for the Huai River guiding project. The preliminary work focuses on surveying. Zhuang Songfu, the vice chairman, and others have completed the survey of the Hongze Lake area in the lower reaches of the Huai River. If the funds for guiding the Huai River can be raised, construction can begin within this year. The committee recently drilled and tested the soil near Jiangba, pre-set an active dam, and increased the number of survey teams to select a route to the sea from near Matouzhen. Water level stations, flow rate stations, and rainfall stations have been set up at important locations along the upper and lower reaches of the Huai River and its tributaries. Each station is equipped with a recorder to record water volume, flow rate, and rainfall. For example, recording the water level uses a water gauge to measure the direction and height of the water level. The water level is observed and recorded every hour from 6:00 am to 6:00 pm every day. The water level is recorded according to the water level recording table. The flow rate is measured using a flow meter to measure the slope and velocity of the water surface and the condition of the riverbed, and the data is recorded in a table. Rainfall is measured using a rain gauge to measure the duration of rainfall from the start of the rain to the end of the rain. The amount of rainfall is recorded in millimeters and recorded in a table, including the number of rainy days in a month and the total monthly rainfall. The water level stations, flow rate stations, and rainfall stations that have been established include Gaoliangjian, Laozi Mountain, Linhuaitou, Xuyi, Qingyangzhen, Sixian, Wuhe, Linhuaiguan, Mingguang, Dingyuan, Bengbu, Huaiyuan, Zhengyangguan, Luan, Huoshan, Fuyang, Taihe, Sanhejian, Honghekou, Xixian, Shangcheng, Guangshan, and more than 20 other locations. Engineer Gui Yefan of the committee came to Bengbu from the lower reaches of the Huai River yesterday (the 3rd) and set up a water level and rainfall station on the main stem of the Huai River in Hebei, appointing Chen Mingqi as the recorder. In addition, Zhuang Songfu, the vice chairman of the committee, and Xu Shiying, a member, arrived in Bengbu by Jinpu train from Nanjing at 4:00 pm on the 4th. The Bengbu General Chamber of Commerce held a welcome meeting at the private Jianghuai Middle School at 6:00 pm on the same day to show their welcome to Zhuang and others who came to Bengbu to inspect the Huai River, which is related to the national economy and people's livelihood. More than 100 people from all walks of life attended. Sun Yuanfu, a member of the Chamber of Commerce, delivered a welcome speech and expressed his hope for the Huai River guiding project. Zhuang Songfu and Xu Shiying then gave speeches and the meeting dispersed at 8:00 pm. At 9:00 am this morning (the 5th), Zhuang and others took a boat to Wuhe, Xuyi and other places to conduct an on-site survey of the depth and situation of the Huai River. After the completion, they will return to Bengbu immediately. (5th)

The Management Rights of the Jichang Railway Amidst the Sino-Japanese Conference

Japanese Representatives Arbitrarily Increase Employee Salaries

Our Railway Authorities Lodge a Protest

Shenyang Correspondence: The Sino-Japanese railway issue was scheduled to be discussed at the end of last month, but because Gao Jiyi, a key person in charge on our side, remained in Tianjin due to business and did not return, Kimura and other special commissioners from the Japanese side recently traveled to Dayun and then returned to Lushun. Therefore, the date of the meeting has not yet been determined. Guo Xurun, the director of the Jichang and Jidun Railway Bureaus, the special commissioner on our side, went to Beiping a few days ago to meet with Vice Commander Zhang and Chairman Gao to report on the situation discussed by the special commissioners in Shenyang every day and to request instructions on the exact date for the start of the meeting with the Japanese side. As for whether the future of the meeting can achieve a mutually beneficial solution to the long-standing cases of the four railways with loan relations with Japan, it depends on the following two points: First, the people of our country must unite to support the authorities. Second, our responsible special commissioners must identify the scope of negotiation and strive to fight. The people of the Northeast have noticed this and have convened meetings of various groups and schools to determine monitoring methods, issue telegrams to the whole country requesting assistance, warn our special commissioners, and meet with the authorities to state public opinion. However, at the time when the meeting is about to open, the Japanese side has suddenly increased the salaries of employees of the Jichang Railway, which originally had a loan relationship. It is heard that our side has lodged a serious protest with the Japanese side due to the fact that rights and interests are at stake, and has requested instructions from the Transportation Committee. The visit of Guo Xurun, the director of the Jichang Railway Bureau, to Beiping is very related to this matter. It is found that the Jichang Railway's loan relationship with Japan was the beginning of the Eastern Provinces Railway. The Eastern Provinces Railway, such as the Jichang, Jidun, Sitao, Taoang, and Siliu Railways, are all railway assets of the Japanese. After the completion of the Eastern Qing Railway, the Russians wanted to extend the Jichang Railway. Changshun, the General of Jilin, planned to raise funds to build it himself and requested permission from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in the 28th year of Guangxu. Russia still made various demands, so he followed his request and changed to the China Eastern Railway Company to undertake the project. After the Russo-Japanese War, Dagui, the General of Jilin, again planned to build it himself, but the Japanese government again used the pretext of recovering the Xinwan Railway to demand the continuation of the Russian construction. Therefore, on the third day of the third month of the 33rd year of Guangxu, the Sino-Japanese Xinwan Jichang Railway Agreement was established, stipulating that half of the funds needed for the self-managed Jichang Railway in China must be borrowed from the Manchurian Railway Company. This was the beginning of our country borrowing Japanese funds to build railways. The Jichang Railway is 79 miles long, equivalent to 125 kilometers. The first loan was made on October 19th of the 34th year of Guangxu, which is November 12th of the 41st year of Meiji. According to the continued agreement sealed, the South Manchurian Railway Company lent 2.15 million Japanese yen. The second loan was made in October of the 6th year of the Republic of China, which is October of the 6th year of Taisho. According to Article 7 of the South Manchurian Inner Mongolia Treaty agreed between the Chinese and Japanese governments on May 25th of the 4th year of the Republic of China, the Minister of Finance and the Minister of Communications, representing the Chinese government, revised the Jichang Railway Loan Contract with the South Manchurian Railway Company. At that time, 4.51125 million Japanese yen was borrowed. After deducting some repayments from the first loan, the combined loan amount was 6.5 million Japanese yen. The actual received price of the loan was 91.50 yen per 100 yen, totaling 4,127,793.75 yen. The loan interest rate was 5 per cent per annum, and the repayment period was 30 years, divided into 40 equal installments. Interest was paid every six months. The management rights of the entire railway belonged to the Chinese government. At that time, due to the outstanding performance of the South Manchurian Railway Company in operating railway business, it was entrusted to direct and manage the business on its behalf during the loan period. Due to the above loan relationship, important officials such as the directors of the three key departments of engineering, accounting, and transportation were all appointed by the Japanese, and one of them was selected as the company representative. However, the salaries of the above officials were to be agreed upon by both parties. Afterwards, Japanese officials took advantage of the situation to control everything, and the rights of our director were almost completely stripped away. Our Chinese employees did not try to resist, and were fooled by the Japanese, only seeking to survive. Although there were a few enlightened staff members who could not fight against them, the railway was only 79 miles long, with an annual turnover of only about 3 million. The simplicity of its business can be seen in general, but the railway has many employees, with about 700 staff and about 200 employees. Road workers are still on the outside, among which Japanese nationals account for

Page 10

a majority. This year, in order to reduce expenditure, our director has strongly advocated reducing the number of employees and is now planning to implement salary reductions to save money. However, not long after, the Japanese side actually unilaterally increased the salaries of Japanese employees. Recently, the Japanese government has been trying to reduce the salaries of its domestic railway employees, and the South Manchurian Railway has also reduced salaries this year. Why is it that the Jichang Railway, which is barely surviving, is being given a raise? Moreover, the contract stipulates that the appointment, removal, promotion, and salary of Chinese and Japanese employees must be agreed upon. The Chinese director proposes the Chinese employees, and the company representative proposes the Japanese employees. It is clearly stipulated. Today's arbitrary salary increase is a violation of the agreement. Therefore, our side has now lodged a serious protest. (June 2)

Preparations for the Representative Assembly of Various Counties in Jiangsu Province

Thirty-Nine Counties, Including Jiangning and Jurong, Have Scheduled Meetings. The Number of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members and the Election Method Have Also Been Specified.

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The lower-level Party branches in various counties in this province were previously stipulated by the Provincial Party Affairs Reorganization Committee to be organized by May 15. It is now learned that according to the statistics of the Organization Section of the Committee, except for a few counties such as Ganyu, Siyang, Yizheng, and Nanhui, where the reorganization of the county Party branches has been delayed, the rest have reported the establishment of the organization or are in the process of re-election, and are actively engaged in the division of the scope of activities of Party members, guiding their activities according to the Guidelines for Party Member Work promulgated by the province. The Committee has formulated a period for holding the first batch of county or district representative assemblies based on the reports of the county Party branches and the inspectors of various districts, and has issued a notice to various counties to follow the schedule after consultation with the inspectors. Wuhu Quick Dispatch

Anhui Provincial Government Chairman Chen Diaoyuan has recently repeatedly requested resignation from the central government due to the difficulty of government finances. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, considering the current turbulent situation, deemed it inappropriate to easily make changes and did not approve the request. Therefore, Chen returned to Anhui from Nanjing this morning on a special boat. Military and political circles here received the news and waited at the riverbank this afternoon to meet him.

Wuhu is located on the Yangtze River and is an important trading port. Its market is the leading town in Anhui. However, the land and property in the prosperous streets are mostly owned by Mr. Li Bohang and the Catholic Church. The Catholic Church's purpose is to spread religion, but it extensively buys properties to collect rent for profit. Shops and residences around Jihe Street and Hongqiangyuan are almost entirely controlled by the church. In the past, officials and civilians did not pay attention to this. Recently, the Wuhu County Government, following the provincial government's order to strictly prohibit foreigners and religious groups from purchasing properties, repeatedly notified the church to report the actual numbers in detail for verification and recovery. However, the church delayed and ignored the order. Therefore, yesterday, an official notice was reissued, requiring the church to investigate and report to the county government for registration within ten days, and to notify the merchants and residents renting the church's properties to report themselves for price assessment and gradual sale. Any surplus funds will be used for local public welfare. The third administrative conference of the county held its second general meeting yesterday, resolving to organize the Wuhu County Local Public Property Clearance Committee, collect public welfare donations for electric light poles and wires, and reorganize the county's grain storage, among other matters. The meeting will continue today.

The National Government promulgated the Provisional Constitution on June 1st. Various circles here held a celebration meeting at the Star Film Theater. The County Chamber of Commerce also scheduled a banquet at First Spring at 4 PM today, inviting military leader Brigadier General Wang, various committee members of the Kuomintang, the Chief of Public Security Bureau, the County Magistrate, and the Customs Superintendent to celebrate the promulgation of the Provisional Constitution. Delegates to the National Assembly, Tao Yutang and She Ceqin, were invited to speak about the National Assembly's proceedings.

The boundary dispute between Anhui and Zhejiang provinces involving the four counties of Jixi, Changhua, Xiuning, and Kaihua has been investigated by Anhui, Zhejiang, and the Ministry of Interior. The Executive Yuan recently decided to redraw the boundaries. The Anhui Provincial Government was ordered to comply. The new boundary between Zhejiang's Changhua and Anhui's Jixi should be delineated with the entire Shangtang Village assigned to Zhejiang, the entire Jingzhou Village assigned to Anhui, the Jiling Mountains to the west as the boundary, the Huishiling watershed to the northeast as the boundary, and the Langguangling mountain range in the middle as the boundary. The new boundary line between Anhui's Xiuning and Zhejiang should follow the center of the stream in the Xikengyuan valley. (3rd)

Local Communications

Local News

Request to Exempt Taxes on Destroyed Fields: A large area of farmland in Wanggongtang and Sanzhao, outside this county's town, was destroyed by the great tide last year, making it difficult to cultivate. The farmers have suffered significant losses. The Fourth District Office has resolved that since the land is not cultivable, it should be treated as undeveloped land and requested that the newly raised taxes be exempted. Landowners should quickly report the details of the damaged fields, grain strings, and field certificate names to the district for forwarding.

Investigating a Case of a Bandit Impersonating the Chief of the Anti-Smuggling Team: Gong Yanzi, a bandit in this county, has repeatedly committed kidnapping and robbery. He has not been apprehended despite numerous attempts. A person recently reported to the county government that Gong is currently the chief of a certain anti-smuggling team in Kunshan. Upon receiving the report, the county government immediately sent a secret letter to the anti-smuggling team, requesting the immediate detention of Gong. Yesterday, confirmation was received that Gong has been arrested. The county government has sent personnel to escort him back for interrogation.

Songjiang

Sea Pirates Handed Over to the Command Headquarters for Interrogation: Today, the bandit suppression command headquarters of Jinshan, Songjiang, Jiading, and Pinghu counties received six sea pirates—Wang Qingfu, Dong Guomin, Jin Shunxiang, Chen Zhuozhao, Lin Shuhai, and Wang Laosi—and one Wang Shaochuan apprehended by the Shanghai Water Police for the Fujian Maritime Patrol of the Zhejiang Fisheries Administration. They have been detained pending interrogation.

Kidnapper Qi A'san Escorted Back to Songjiang: As previously reported, the first squad of the county police team opened fire on bandits in Wuquekou on the morning of the 4th. Suspecting that kidnappers Qi A'yun and others had returned to their hometown to hide, they planned a surprise arrest. However, the bandits became aware and opened fire, leading to intense fighting. Qi A'yun and others managed to escape by diving into the water. Qi A'san (nicknamed Tongtian A'san) was captured and is being escorted back for interrogation.

Suzhou

Water Police Detectives Arrest Bandits in Suzhou: Huang Dianqing, a detective from the 11th team of the 3rd district of the Suzhou Water Police, together with Cheng Zeyou, a detective from the 14th team, came from Wujiang last night (the 5th) based on information that bandits from Henan were hiding in Suzhou. Huang and Cheng, along with police officers from the 2nd sub-bureau of the 3rd branch of the Public Security Bureau, arrested Chen Xiliang, a bandit from Hunan, at Taoyuanfang on the road outside Changmen at around 10 PM that night. Another bandit escaped. 171 silver dollars and silver chains were found on Chen, who was immediately taken to the 2nd sub-bureau and transferred to the 3rd branch. Yesterday, the 3rd district of the Water Police took him for investigation.

Kidnapping Case at Nanbeiqiao: Victims Escape: Xu Nanchen and other families from Yaojiabang village in Nanbeiqiao were previously robbed and kidnapped. Xu's second and third sons, Xu Ruichen's son Rongsheng, and Lu Gunguan, Lu A'mao, Chen Shuncheng, and Lu A'bao from Lujiali village, have not been ransomed. It is now known that Lu A'mao and Lu Gunguan escaped a few days ago. However, the five Xu children are still in danger.

Wuxi

Exhumation of a Child Bride for Autopsy: Lu, the daughter of Lu A'xiao from Luxiang, Xuedian township, in the 572nd Tu of the 12th district of this county, was married to Qian A'ding's son. Qian's son was a tailor in Hankou. On May 29th, Lu suddenly disappeared without saying goodbye. Her father-in-law suspected she went to her mother's house. However, on the 2nd of this month, her body was found in the Taojiabang River. The families on both sides recovered the body and prepared a coffin for burial, while also telegramming Qian's son to return home. Cao Hongshou, the Tu leader, reported the case to the county court as it involved a death. Yesterday, Prosecutor Du went to the village. Because Lu A'xiao refused to take responsibility for a waiver of autopsy, the coffin was immediately opened for autopsy. The body was already decomposed. The autopsy revealed that she had fallen into the river and drowned, with no injuries. Qian A'ding was ordered to re-coffin and bury the body.

Aftermath of the Competition for the Pacific Factory: The buildings and foundations of the Pacific Soap Factory on Xiaojianshang, west of the city, were previously subject to competition between Shen Guiqing and Tao Yinpu, who were engaged in the rice and wheat business. Initially, it was a civil lawsuit that lasted for half a year without resolution. Subsequently, a brawl occurred, and both parties went to the county court for injury verification, resulting in a criminal prosecution followed by detention. During the court's interrogation, both parties made concessions and withdrew the charges, reverting to civil proceedings. Afterwards, a Mr. Gu filed a complaint with the Suzhou High Court, alleging that the parties involved in the case had bribed officials and requested a thorough investigation to uphold the rule of law. Yesterday, the High Court appointed Prosecutor Jin Henian to investigate the case in Wuxi. A summons was issued in advance to more than ten people involved in the case, including Tao Peiji. After arriving in Wuxi, Prosecutor Jin went directly to the court to open an investigation hearing. Those who were summoned and arrived were Tao Binyu, Lu Tao'an, Shen Guiqing, and Yang Lubing. After careful interrogation, all claimed that they had not engaged in bribery. As a result, each person was ordered to sign the record and instructed to bring the statements to Suzhou for further orders.

Water Police Detectives Seize Guns While Apprehending Bandits: Chen Hanrong, the captain of the Water Police's 2nd District Detective Team, previously received information that bandits were hiding in Wuxing County and had guns hidden in the Shikeng. He immediately reported to District Chief Mao and prepared a document to Wuxing County for investigation. A few days ago, he coordinated with the chief of the Public Security Bureau of that county and rushed to a village about eight miles from the city. They seized a Mauser rifle in an earthen pit. However, the bandits had already fled upon hearing the news. He immediately returned to Wuxi with the firearm yesterday to report and investigate the whereabouts of the remaining bandits.

Illegally Imprisoning His Wife with Iron Chains: Transferred to Hospital for Legal Action: The Public Security Bureau's 4th branch received a report from a woman, Lu Wang, that her daughter, who had married Liu Baozhen, a tea shop owner in Quanting, Huishan, had been imprisoned with iron chains due to Liu's affair. She had suffered injuries all over her body and requested police assistance. Upon receiving the report, the bureau dispatched Patrolman Wang Zhenbin from the 1st police station, along with the Tu leader, to the scene. At the Yilantang, they found Liu Lu locked in a room. Liu Baozhen, along with his shop assistants Mazi A'bing, Lengzi Hui, Bing Jiangbei A'san, and other five people, were taken to the bureau for a brief interrogation before being transferred to the General Bureau. Yesterday, Wang Zhonghu, the chief of the 3rd section, interrogated them and ordered the defendant, Liu Baozhen, to pay 120 silver dollars to send his wife to a mental hospital in Suzhou for treatment. However, the defendant disobeyed and continued to imprison and beat his wife, withholding food. A request was made to transfer the case to the hospital for legal action. During the interrogation, Liu Lu stated that her husband had an affair and claimed she was mentally ill to justify the imprisonment and withholding of food. She also stated that he ordered his assistants to beat her. While speaking, she gesticulated wildly, showing signs of mental instability. The iron chains on her feet had not yet been removed. Liu Baozhen stated that Lu had been ill last year and had gone crazy after recovering. Recently, her condition had worsened, and she often caused trouble outside, so he was forced to lock her up to prevent accidents. Mazi and A'bing stated that they indeed helped with the imprisonment but did not beat her. Chief Wang verified the statements and, since the case had been filed with the county court, ordered that it be transferred to the hospital for legal action.

Changzhou

Bandit Chen Genda Executed by Firing Squad: Zhang Pengzhu, the county magistrate and chief of the Cleansing Bureau of Wujin County, previously apprehended a bandit named Lu Genda. Based on his confession of robbery and extortion, he was sentenced to death. The provincial government approved the execution by telegram. County Magistrate Zhang dispatched police to escort the bandit to the execution ground at Fengweidun at 7 AM on the 6th to verify his identity and execute the firing squad.

Shengang Vessel Robbed En Route: A Shengang vessel from Jiangyin was sailing near Yuanjiacun in the Hekou area of Wujin when suddenly seven or eight bandits armed with flashlights and pistols opened fire on the ship as a warning. They boarded the ship and robbed all the passengers and cargo, causing losses of about 500-600 silver dollars. The shipowner reported the incident to the Shipping Association, which reported it to the county government on the 5th, requesting the apprehension of the bandits and the recovery of the stolen goods.

Jiangyin

Gong Hao of Zhouzhuang Kidnapped in Hubei: Gong Hao, from Gong Peng village, Zhouzhuang, was a scout instructor at the Provincial 14th Middle School in Hubei Province. On April 16th, when Jingmen fell, four faculty members were killed, and six were kidnapped, including Gong. Forty to fifty students were also kidnapped. The family of Gong was informed by a letter from Shan Bingkang, a physical education teacher at Hanyang Middle School.

Jurong

Bandit Drowns After Being Shot by Police: The Provincial Security Team stationed at Yuntang Temple in Beixiang was patrolling in the area around Dashanjiao, Shiqian Village. They spotted three people who appeared to be bandits and pursued them until they reached a dense forest behind Yujia Mountain Village. One bandit, with no way to escape, quickly hid in a pond, covering his head with aquatic plants. However, a soldier spotted him and shot him. The other two bandits hid in the forest and were not found.

Zhenjiang

Seven Bandits from Dongtai Escorted to the Province: Huang Cishan, the county magistrate of Dongtai, yesterday dispatched police to escort seven bandits and suspects—Tao Xuezhong, Bian Changxue, Zhang Dianlong, Tao Wenqing, Xu Huaiyi, Xu Yinshan, and Tao Xuesheng—to the province. A document was sent to the Security Office for transfer to the special operations battalion for supervision. After questioning by Battalion Commander Shen, a team was dispatched to transfer the bandits to the Military Law Section of the Security Office for strict handling according to the law.

Gaoyou

Farmer Struck and Killed by Lightning: Jiang Xiaohuzi, a 26-year-old farmer from Guijiazhuang Village, Shibao Township, was transplanting rice seedlings in the field with more than 20 companions on the afternoon of the day before yesterday (the 3rd) during a heavy rainstorm. Suddenly, a lightning strike killed Jiang Xiaohuzi. It was a tragic incident.

Grain Ship Narrowly Escapes Robbery at Huajiatan: A grain merchant, Pan Hongfu, purchased miscellaneous grains in Jiangba Town, Xuyi County, and loaded them onto a ship for sale in Gaoyou. However, yesterday (the 3rd) at 1 PM, when the ship reached Huajiatan in Baoying County, it was suddenly pursued by a bandit ship that fired shots from behind. At that time, Liu Qindian, the captain of the Hongze Lake patrol team, was passing by on his way to the Sixth District Department in Youyao. Hearing the gunshots, he fired back to investigate. The bandits fled north upon seeing the police team. Captain Liu then escorted Pan's ship to Gaoyou.

Nantong

Forced Demolition of Civil Housing Along the City Walls: The Education Bureau released city wall land for rent to raise education funds. The bureau investigated and found that more than thirty households had encroached on the land and received approval from the county government to relocate them within one month. As the deadline has passed, County Magistrate Zhang has ordered the Public Security Bureau to dispatch police to forcibly carry out the relocation.

Resolution on the Ownership of the Poor People's Workshop: The various sectors of Nantong originally intended to transform the Poor People's Workshop west of the city into a vocational training center for vagrants. Later, the 11th Division of the Army took over the workshop and used it as a vocational training factory for wounded soldiers. Various sectors petitioned Chang Xiaoruo, the chairman of the workshop, to appeal to the headquarters for clarification of the property rights. A telegram was received approving the 11th Division to select another site, and the Poor People's Workshop would remain for local public use. The case of the body thrown off the Dahe Wheelship is to be heard in Zhenjiang. Ge Tianliang and 63 other people from Nantong filed a petition with the county government requesting a thorough investigation of the case of a body thrown off the Dahe Wheelship at Tianshenggang. County Magistrate Zhang stated that the High Court had ordered the case to be transferred to the Zhenjiang District Court for trial, and the witnesses were awaiting the court date. Since the case had been returned to the judiciary, it should be resolved by the court.

Yixing

District Party Committee Member Arrested on Suspicion of Being a Reactionary: Chu Guoying, a standing committee member of the Yixing County District Party Committee, was suddenly arrested yesterday by Wu, the chief of the County Public Security Bureau, on suspicion of being a reactionary. According to party officials, he was falsely accused by Ge Ziqing, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, who was protecting Yan, whose misdeeds of gambling were well-known. Chu Guoying, a standing committee member of the district party committee, repeatedly criticized him. Yan, harboring resentment, colluded with opponents of Chu to forge reactionary letters, which were mailed from Liyang to Chu. The bureau chief anticipated the arrival of the letter and dispatched police to check the mail, seizing the letter and sending it to the county government by telephone. It is said that the county government refused to accept it due to the lack of evidence. However, the County Party Rectification Committee opposed the Public Security Bureau's unauthorized arrest of a committee member without notifying the senior party organization.

Jiaxing

Resolution of the Boundary Issue Between Jiaxing and Haiyan Counties: The issue of boundary demarcation between Jiaxing and Haiyan counties had been discussed several times, but it was halted due to the public's dissatisfaction. Recently, the county governments of the two counties received an order from the province to reconvene the related villages and experienced gentry on both sides to resolve the issue as soon as possible. On the 4th, the two county governments convened a meeting of the related villages and local figures at Shenbo Town, which is located on the border of Jiaxing and Haiyan, to discuss the matter. After discussion, it was decided that the convenience of agricultural production and sales should be the guiding principle, and the original county boundaries should be the standard. The boundary lines between Dayishiyi village of Jiaxing and Weizi village of Haiyan, as well as Buchun village and Chucun of Haiyan and Dayishiyi, Er villages of Jiaxing, and Dongnan village of Jiaxing and Shuangcun village of Haiyan, will follow the original natural boundaries. If there are any ambiguities due to intertwining boundaries, the village committees of both sides will jointly investigate, make artificial modifications, and establish boundary markers. Both sides agreed to the decision. The fifth district chief of Jiaxing, Zhu Jipan, the sixth district chief of Haiyan, Xu Yizhi, and the representatives of the meeting signed the documents and submitted them to the county for review and approval by the province.

Pinghu

Appeal of the Case of Tang Lianfu's Unexplained Death: After Tang Lianfu, hired by Shen Heshang, a Qing civilian outside the Dananmen, went missing in April of last year, his younger brother Shunfu discovered Tang Lianfu's body in the Lidunfang River two days later. The family's investigation revealed that Shen Heshang was suspected of inciting Qian A'er, Shen Shengchang, and Ni A'jiu to murder Tang. They filed a lawsuit with the county government, requesting investigation and legal action. After the county government examined the body and conducted multiple investigations and interrogations, it was declared that there was insufficient evidence to prove that Shen Heshang and Qian A'er were guilty of Tang Lianfu's unexplained death. Shen A'jiu, Ni A'liu, and Shen Shengchang were still suspects, and further investigation would be conducted. The plaintiff did not accept the verdict and hired a lawyer to appeal to the Hangzhou High Court, which is scheduled to convene on the 12th of this month.

Hengli Silk Factory Burnt Down in a Fire: The Hengli Silk Factory in Chaonitan was accidentally burned down yesterday in the middle of the night due to improper cocoon drying, resulting in significant losses. It is reported that the factory has fire insurance and has reported to the insurance company for verification and compensation.

Hangzhou

Child Crushed to Death by Train from Shanghai to Hangzhou: At 9:50 AM yesterday morning, the Number 3 train from Shanghai to Ningbo was traveling from Zhakou to Shanghai when, near Caoqiaomen, a minor child was playing. He was unable to avoid the train in time and was crushed to death, a gruesome sight.

Four More Fugitive Bandits from Shiwan Captured: Jiang Boxiong, the chief of the Third District of the Water Police stationed in Nanxun, received a report that a large number of fugitive bandits from Shiwan were hiding in Xujiazhuang, Xinshi. He immediately coordinated with the Second Regiment of the Security Force to dispatch a team to the area. The bandits were caught off guard, and Cai Yatou, Chen Baotang, Cai Zhaoxin, and Cai Jinbao were captured. Five bandit guns and more than ten catties of stolen silver were found in a shed. They were escorted and transferred to the local county Cleansing Bureau. A telegram was sent to the province to report the situation.

Ningbo

Major Fire in Lishi Town: Yesterday (the 4th) at 11 AM, a fire broke out in Teng Laoshun's house near the Chongfu Temple in Lishi Town, Yin County, due to careless cooking. The smoke quickly spread, and the fire became intense. It took more than two hours to extinguish the fire, which destroyed 34 houses and affected 32 families. Teng Laoshun suffered severe burns to the head and was taken to Huamei Hospital for treatment.

Taizhou

Notorious Bandit Shan Laofang Arrested: Shan Laofang, a notorious bandit from Linhai, had committed numerous crimes of kidnapping and extortion in various villages of the county. The authorities had ordered his arrest many times, but he had not been apprehended. It was learned that the notorious bandit had mixed into the cattle market outside the East Gate, three miles from the city, a few days ago. The battalion headquarters of the 1st Battalion of the 5th Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Force stationed in the city learned of this and dispatched four plainclothes soldiers to the scene to arrest the bandit. He was immediately taken to the battalion headquarters and transferred to the local judicial sub-court for interrogation.

Education News

Important News

Split in the Tsinghua Turmoil

Nanjing, 6th (Central News Agency) The Ministry of Education issued instructions on the 6th to Wu Nanxuan, the president of Tsinghua University, to take active responsibility and not consider resigning.

Beiping, 6th (Telegram) The Tsinghua Student Self-Government Association resolved on the evening of the 5th to adhere to the principles of safeguarding the university and firmly expelling Wu Nanxuan.

Education Circles in Beijing and Shanghai Agree on June 6 as Teachers' Day

Organizing a Teachers' Association

Nanjing, 6th (Telegram) Over 300 people from education circles in Beijing and Shanghai celebrated Teachers' Day at the Central University and resolved to request the National Government to formally designate June 6 as Teachers' Day. They also resolved to organize a National Teachers' Association and elected Tai Shuangqiu, Ma Ketan, and 13 others as organizers.

Ministry of Education Appeals to Retain Zhejiang Education Commissioner

But Zhang Daofan Insists on Resigning in Beijing

Zhang Daofan, the Education Commissioner of Zhejiang, had previously submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Education due to the financial difficulties of the provincial education budget. The Ministry of Education believed that Zhejiang's education relied on him to preside over it and did not approve his request. It has now issued an appeal to retain him. The original order is as follows: "Having reviewed the submission, the Commissioner has spared no effort in planning and reorganizing since taking office, and his diligence and outstanding work are deeply valued and relied upon. At present, Zhejiang's education needs to be actively developed to achieve complete success. It is hoped that he will avoid difficulty and not consider resigning. The request to submit his resignation should not be discussed. In addition to submitting a separate document to the Executive Yuan for review and filing, and consulting with the Zhejiang Provincial Government to find ways to raise and distribute overdue education funds to facilitate progress, you are still expected to continue your efforts to emphasize education. This is the order."

Furthermore, it is reported that Mr. Zhang's intention to resign is firm. Fearing that he would not be able to obtain central approval soon, he went to Beijing a few days ago to personally present his resignation in the hope of receiving an early approval.

Five Private Universities Request Subsidies

Nanjing, 6th (Telegram) The five universities, including the Private Chaoyang University, Cultural Populace University, North China University, and Zhonghua University, jointly submitted a request to the National Government to subsidize each school with 20,000 yuan per month from Russian funds, following the examples of the Private Sino-French University and China College. It has been sent to the Executive Yuan for processing.

Sports

Jiang-Zhe Middle School Tennis Championship Title to be Decided Tomorrow

Shanghai vs. Soochow

Loser's Championship Set for the Day After Johnson Forfeits

Yesterday was the second day of the Zhejiang Private Middle School Tennis Tournament. According to the original schedule, the semi-final rematch between Johnson and Yan Chengzhi was scheduled for 8:30 AM, and the final between Soochow and the winner of the Yan Chengzhi group was scheduled for 4:15 PM to determine the championship. However, during the match between Johnson and Yan Chengzhi, Johnson's Western coach, Bu Xun, arrived and claimed that he had just heard news of a dispute in the competition. Although Johnson had won the rematch the day before, he personally felt deeply regretful about the matter, as the distribution of players before and after the game was indeed inappropriate and violated the rules of the tournament. He wished to formally declare his forfeiture to the tournament. The president, Wang Bingjian, believed that since the situation was already a fait accompli and Coach Bu was willing to forfeit to preserve sportsmanship, it was a good thing. Therefore, he ordered the suspension of the match between Yan Chengzhi and Johnson and restored the right to the rematch for Shanghai. The issue of the championship became even more uncertain.

Shanghai Defeats Yan Chengzhi

At 4:15 PM in the afternoon, Yan Chengzhi and Shanghai held a rematch at Taowu Stadium. As a result, Shanghai won 3-0 and secured the right to the final.

In the first singles match, Yu Tianguang of Shanghai faced Dai Guangjin of Yan Chengzhi. Yu, known for his prowess in Shanghai, had a good chance of winning, but he was too aggressive and made many mistakes. He lost the second set due to this. Dai was careful and cautious, but still lost the third set. It was an unavoidable fate. The referee was Ni Guoliang. The score was as follows:

Shanghai Yu Tianguang 6-4, 3-6, 6-1 Yan Chengzhi Dai Guangjin

In the second singles match, Xu Zenrui of Shanghai faced Huang Hanzhu of Yan Chengzhi. Huang Hanzhu's performance was lackluster. Xu Zenrui's effective attacks were the foundation of his victory. The referee was Huang Bingjian.

Shanghai Xu Zenrui 4-6, 6-0, 6-0 Yan Chengzhi Huang Hanzhu

In the third singles match, Xu Zengguang of Shanghai faced Zhu Zichang of Yan Chengzhi. The strengths of the two sides were comparable. The score fluctuated in each game, also very close. However, Xu's ball was low and moving, making it difficult to defend. He was defeated as a result. The referee was Mei Naikui.

Shanghai Xu Zengguang 4-6, 6-7, 7-5 Yan Chengzhi Zhu Zichang

Championship Awaits Tomorrow

The championship match is now scheduled for 4 PM on Monday at Taowu. The participants in the final are Soochow and Shanghai. The championship match has been changed to the 9th.

Shanghai Banking Club Billiards Finals Tomorrow Night

Li Gongying vs. Shen Lince

The Shanghai Banking Club has perfect facilities and thriving affairs. This year, considering that many members rarely have the opportunity to exercise due to their job duties, they rented a tennis court and established a tennis club. It is said that quite a few members have joined. Last month, they held a billiards handicap competition as usual, with 28 people participating. The finals are scheduled for tomorrow (June 8th) at 6:00 PM in the club's billiards room. The finalists are Li Gongying and Shen Lince. Mr. Li won the Shanghai Senior Billiards Association championship last year, creating a new record for Chinese people winning that championship. His billiards skills are naturally outstanding. Mr. Shen is also an expert. Although this handicap competition allowed him to score 700 points, he was able to fight his way to victory and participate in the finals. Therefore, it is unknown who will win on that night. A crowd of seventeen people stepped forward. The Chinese Zhang Hugen took the lead, refreshing and fast, leading the way. Dong Jiaxie followed. Remidy and Sugden chased behind, and Chen Xingpei followed closely behind Remidy. In the second lap, at the halfway point of 700 meters, Remidy and Sugden were still comfortably following behind. After 1000 meters, Lei Su's footsteps accelerated as they flew, catching up to Zhang and Dong. But one was rising, and the other was exhausted. So it was known that Zhang and Dong were in danger. Gradually falling behind and farther away, in the last 200 meters, Lei Su both charged fiercely. Sugden rushed out about three meters ahead of Remidius at 80 meters from the finish line and won first place. Truelock came in third, and Harletai caught up, with Qiu Lingru taking fourth place. The result of 4 minutes and 11.94 seconds was very satisfying.

Unexpected Failure of Chinese in the Discus Throw

The discus throw results were mediocre. There were few outstanding athletes among the sixteen people. 32.83 meters Wang Jihuai and Chen Baoqiu could both achieve this number. The farthest the two threw was only around 30 meters. The referee Shen Kunnan said that they were nervous on the field and the discus went out too high, so the landing point was close. Initially, the German Kramer had just over 32 meters. Seeing the German flag planted, the others sighed. Although Tomaszewski participated in the open qualifying competition and was counted, Wang Chen was still disappointed in the last throw, which can be said to be an unexpected loss. Kubin's last throw won him first place. It was really lucky.

The Frustrating Long Jump Final

Before the last five minutes of the long jump, it was still completely dominated by the Chinese. The Chinese occupied the top one, two, three, four, and five spots. Wang Jihuai was leading with 6.40 meters. Who knew that in the sixth jump, Schwank jumped 6.46 meters, overtaking Wang Jihuai. This 0.06 meters caused the Chinese to lose all their efforts. The results were still acceptable.

Li Zhongsan's Worries in the High Jump

Fifteen people competed in the high jump, gradually eliminating each other. Li Lin steadily sat in fifth place with 1.68 meters. Gu Huo then jumped over 1.72 meters, sitting in fourth place. Li Zhongsan, Anderson, and the Japanese Furukawa competed for the top three. Up to 1.76 meters, Li Zhongsan passed, and Furukawa also passed. Anderson also passed on the third try. Adding one,

If he could pass 1.82 meters, it would be a new national record. Li jumped and failed, and everyone was worried. Furukawa and Anderson also failed, which was very comforting. Then he lowered one level to five feet eleven. Li failed to pass, and Furukawa and the two also failed to pass. Then he retreated to five feet ten. Li passed, and Gu An failed. Li then won the championship. At five feet eight, Gu (one jump) Furukawa failed, and Anderson took second place.

Great Pity in the 400 Meter Relay

The Chinese team had good talent in the 400-meter relay. In the first leg, Zhong Lianji surpassed the American Mario by a lot. In the second leg, Zhou Ende was even farther ahead. Bernett could not catch up. However, Zhou's handoff to the third leg, Hao Chunde, was not coordinated. Schwank jumped ahead, and Lin Xing had no way to catch Thurlow. It was a great pity.

Thurlow easily ran the first place in the 100 meters and 200 meters, looking at the second-place runner while the results were the best. The final is very likely to win. In the 400 meters, Thurlow did not exert effort, only vying for a position to prepare for today's competition. Lin Guangxing did not have any special features, perhaps because of the preliminary round. Zhou Ende may have hope in the 200 meters. Gu Zaiping finished third in the third heat of the 100 meters and had cramps at the finish line, giving up the 200 meters. Chinese people really need to work hard in the short distances, otherwise it is dangerous and perilous. In the high hurdles, Schwank and Furukawa cannot be ignored.
