Free Talk

A Word or Two

— Holding the Buddha

Crying is the most enjoyable thing in life, especially for lovers.

It is better to cry together in poverty than to hear a lion's roar in wealth.

A cheerful disposition, passionate emotions, a peaceful ambition, and a pure and beautiful appearance: this is my ideal of a beautiful woman.

Can a beautiful woman be made by combining Xiangyun's cheerfulness, Miaoyu's peace, and Daiyu's purity? Otherwise, it is impossible to find a beautiful woman even in the Grand View Garden, let alone elsewhere.

Among vernacular love novels, Dream of the Red Chamber is the best. Among classical Chinese love novels, Broken Qin Building is the best. Aside from Haggard and the Dumas father and son, Xueqin and He Zhou can be called the masters of love novels.

The world's four great religious leaders were all born in peninsulas of the East: Confucius in Shandong, Shakyamuni in India, Muhammad in Arabia, and Jesus in Asia Minor. Therefore, the West will never surpass the East.

Love between the sexes sometimes breaks off, but unrequited love remains unchanged for life and becomes more flavorful over time.

The most beautiful women in the world are those in paintings and books, otherwise there will inevitably be flaws. Therefore, pursuing women is not as good as reading books and looking at paintings.

Record of National Martial Arts

— Songlu

Last year, when the national martial arts competition was held in Hangzhou, I met two or three warriors in my spare time. What we talked about before was all trivial stories about national martial arts, among which there were no lack of heroic and chivalrous deeds that were worth discussing. With nothing to do in the rented window, I wetted my brush and wrote them down.

Traveling upstream along the Qiantang River and turning left, there is a county between Jin and Lan called Yiwu. The local customs are bold and brave, and they like to fight. Every spring and autumn, the locals like to hold god-welcoming and racing events. Many aggressive people take the opportunity to set up gambling tables. Those who come throw away their houses and sell their properties, scraping together everything they have. They do not hesitate to bet thousands of gold coins in one go. One day, a young man in fur clothes and horses came with a servant and threw a pile of gold coins on the table with a clanging sound. The gamblers, all outsiders, were even more happy to gamble with him. In an instant, the young man lost two thousand gold coins and his money bag was empty. He got up, straightened his clothes, and left without any sadness. He came again the next day, bringing even more gold than yesterday, and asked to be the dealer. After only a few throws, he had won more than five thousand gold coins. The young man immediately said, "Stop!" He ordered his servant to take the gold he had won and left proudly. The gamblers, seeing that he was delicate and weak, shouted loudly, "Where are you going, guest? Return the money you won, and you will be forgiven. Otherwise, your life will not be guaranteed. Do you still want to seize our money?" The young man was also angry and did not give in at all. The crowd surrounded him and attacked him. The young man laughed and said, "Do you rats want to rob me by force? Please try my fist." As soon as he waved his hand, those who were hit fell more than ten feet away. The crowd took out iron weapons and attacked him. The young man took out the folding fan he was carrying and blocked them. Those who were hit fell. The crowd knew they could not win and dispersed. The young man said, "You rats have only this much skill and you want to bully people with violence?" After saying this, he laughed wildly and left. Later, someone asked about the young man's name. He was Wang, a successful candidate in the imperial examinations from Shanyin. It was said that Wang had traveled with a strange person since he was young and could pierce solid stones with his fingers. This time, he did not want to hurt people to cause trouble, so he only showed off his skills a little.

There was a boxing master named Jin in Zhuji who had hundreds of students and was a hero in one village. He claimed that he had never met an opponent in his life. One day, a boy came, only fifteen or sixteen years old, bowed and asked, "I heard that you are famous for your bravery and I would like to become your disciple." Jin said, "You are weak and I am afraid that it will not be easy for you to succeed." The boy laughed and said, "However, I have a small skill. Let me entertain my master with it." He lifted a bucket of water in front of the courtyard and poured it into the air, splashing the water more than ten feet. Then he filled the bucket with water again, and all the water went into the bucket without a drop missing. He then chopped down the flagpole in front of the door with a palm. Jin was greatly frightened when he saw this and said, "I did not expect the boy's divine skill to be ten times better than mine." He fled and never became a teacher again. Some say that the boy did not have much skill and only practiced these two things well, but it was also miraculous. It is a pity that the narrator forgot his name.

Recent Events of Edison

— Lvb冰

Almost everyone in the world knows that the greatest inventor is Edison. Last month, his son was in London, and people from all walks of life asked him about the inventor's recent situation. Newspapers and magazines have all recorded it, and I will summarize what I heard below.

Although Mr. Edison is already eighty-four years old, he still works for nine or ten hours every day. When he gets a new and different idea for an invention, he immediately starts experimenting. Even if his family urges him to eat, he turns his head and ignores them. He is in good health and high spirits. He often has at least five or six new ideas in his mind at the same time to solve the problem. He enjoys this kind of life very much.

The thing that Mr. Edison is most interested in now is experimenting to press rubber from the green leaves of plants. Up to now, he has analyzed more than 22,000 kinds of plants. Although he has not completely succeeded, he is still working hard and will eventually realize it one day. Other inventions, such as new-style motorcycles, automatic switches, train lights, electric heaters, electric pots, etc., have all been put into practical use in society. In short, the old man's thinking is old and more acute, and ideas flow from his mind, so his inventions are still endless.

Talking about Baodu Mountain

— Cheng Wuxi

Baodu Mountain is a dangerous mountain northwest of Yixian County, Shandong Province. It originally did not have a prominent name in history, but it became famous after Sun Meiyao's train robbery case in Lincheng. Now it is occupied by Sun Meisong as a bandit den. Why does Baodu Mountain have so much connection with bandits? My friend Mr. Wang, who does business in Yixian County, said that the scenery there is beautiful and it produces many exotic flowers and herbs, making it like a paradise. I have longed for it for a long time. On a boring rainy day, I will describe what he said and submit it to Free Talk to tell the world's mountain and water addicts.

Baodu Mountain was originally named Jun Mountain and is the source of the West Jia River. Legend has it that a hermit embraced a calf and escaped to the top to cultivate it, hence the current name. It is about nine li high and forty-five li in circumference. To the south, it leads Zhuo Mountain on the left and controls Yun Valley Mountain on the right, with doorways in between, and Baiyun Mountain as the welcoming screen. To the east, it guards the solidity of Shen Mountain, and to the west, it occupies the danger of E Mountain. The left wing, Lotus Mountain, has tall peaks arranged in a row for more than ten li, with pine and cypress trees shading the sky. The south side of the mountain is a flat area of six or seven li, and the right palm is covered with the vast Xing Mountain, with strange peaks and ridges crowned with clouds, competing with Lotus Mountain. Below it, the ground is covered with yellow grass, decorated with countless fruit trees. When thousands of flowers bloom at the same time, the five colors are all prepared, making it a spectacle. Below the northern ridge, there is a small path leading to Feixian County, and Zhuoyun Mountain has the same terrain: one man guards the pass, and ten thousand men cannot enter. The mountains surround each other and the waters meet, making it incomparably dangerous. It is indeed a guarantee for the southern border of Shandong Province. The mountains surrounding each other make the environment of Baodu Mountain dangerous, but its own danger is even greater than the environment. From the foot of the mountain to the top, the cliffs are thousands of feet high. In the northwest, the rocks are folded and the steps are chiseled to reach them, allowing only enough space for one foot. The top of the mountain is square and covers an area of dozens of miles, all of which is black soil and can be cultivated. It is covered with thatch. There is a very large stone pool, four or five feet deep, which does not dry up in a severe drought, and there is also a well more than ten feet deep, which is clear, green, sweet, and can be used for drinking. Wild grass extends over the cliffs, with purple stems and green leaves, and their names are not known. They have the effect of treating diseases. Below it, there are plants such as Calophyllum, Zelkova, and bitter lettuce. There are many unnamed small birds with red feathers that sing high in the treetops at dusk, resembling songs. Such a scenic spot has been occupied as a bandit den, making people regard it as a dangerous place. I cannot help but feel emotional about it.

Continued Notes on Germophobia

— Drunkenly Obsessed Student

There are three people I know who have germophobia and are full of quirks. Compared to the Shi and Yan you described, they are probably more extreme. I will list them below to make you laugh.

A friend of Mr. Cheng has a relative called Old Miss, who is old but still unmarried. People call her Old Miss. Old Miss is a germaphobe and always takes on the cleaning of her room herself. She does not like to use servants. She requires that everything in her room be clean and spotless. If a guest accidentally enters her room, regardless of gender, she will be sure to wipe the chairs and stools they sat on again and again. Not to mention washing the teacups they drank from. People know her quirks, so few people visit her. Old Miss once said that most men and women in the world are dirty, so she is determined not to marry and would rather remain a spinster.

There is a Mr. Lu in the South Market who is over sixty years old and also has germophobia. He pays special attention to his diet. He always declines banquets from relatives and friends. Although there are many restaurants in Shanghai, he rarely sets foot in them, fearing that the food is not clean. He says that only Western food is barely acceptable, but when he patronizes a Western restaurant, he must first ask where the kitchen is and personally visit it to see if its layout is suitable and clean. If it meets his requirements, he will stay; if not, he will turn his head and leave and go to another restaurant, even if it means traveling a long distance. Therefore, he knows which kitchens in the Western restaurants in the North Market are clean and hygienic and which are not. As for the kitchens of other miscellaneous restaurants, he says that they are not worth a look. He is too busy avoiding them, so how can he be happy? Such a meticulous eater is rare. Mr. Lu once said to me that he pays attention to hygiene everywhere, so he should be able to avoid diseases and enter the road to health, but he is still sick all his life, which is difficult to understand. I also smiled and replied.

My friend Mr. Ren works in a certain government agency in the capital. A colleague of his is a bachelor and has quirks. He likes to wear new socks every day. He only wears socks once and throws them away if they are slightly dirty and never washes and changes them again. There is a basket in the corner of his room, and the socks he throws away are always piled up like a small hill. It is said that he pays his washing woman a lot of money. The annual cost is quite a lot, so people call him the "Sock King."

A Trip Around the Yellow Sea (24)

— Huang Yanpei

On April 22nd, I boarded a ship from Kobe to return to China. After stopping at Nagasaki for two hours, I left for home. At this time, only a few points remain in my mind.

(1) Japan is able to continue to develop Eastern old culture by using Western new culture. Therefore, on one hand, they show a very large amount of absorption, and on the other hand, they show a very strong conservatism.

(2) Japan's current position is also very dangerous. The situation of confrontation between the two major financial groups has long been formed, and they are each showing their magical powers to use the two major political parties they created with financial resources as a bitter struggle on the political stage. When they encounter common interests, such as dealing with the Communist Party and the Proletarian Party, they temporarily unite. As a result, the confrontation between labor and capital is becoming increasingly fierce. Their national absorption is great, and education is relatively popular, so their so-called ideological problems cannot be solved by high pressure or small patching methods. Their population is increasing at a very high rate. Since the problem of recession occurred, it has further promoted changes in their thinking. As for foreign countries, everyone is paying attention to the impact on Eastern commerce and economy after the completion of the Soviet Union's five-year industrial plan and wants to solve it ahead of time. The problem of irresistible earthquakes occurs on a small scale every few years and on a large scale every few decades. In other nations, this may inevitably lead to ideological sadness and decadence, but they turn it into a motivation for advancement. However, it is also said that the outlook on life of some people has changed as a result. These are all current situations and problems to be solved in their country.

(3) Because of the above, a conclusion is naturally formed into a national consensus: outward development. The ambitions of warlords and capitalists go without saying. Politicians believe that the only way to reduce the entanglement of labor-capital class problems is to use national thought to break through it horizontally. As for the population problem, the economic problem, and even the natural disaster problem, it is nothing more than that Changsha is too small to maneuver. The only way to solve the problem is to develop outward, outward development. Who else is there to develop towards besides us, China? What about the past advocacy of the Japanese-American war, and the current advocacy of the Japanese-Soviet war? Why do they have hatred for the United States and hatred for the Soviet Union? The competition is for us, China. However, their goals are even broader than before. In the past, it was for Manchuria and Mongolia. Now, the entire area north of the Yellow River is within their reach.

Now that we know Japan's present and future, let's discuss our own.

Rotary Club Storytelling

Casual Lake Talks (5)

— Tianxu Wosheng

The title of "Tangguan" (Hall Official) began in the Song Dynasty. During the Chunxi period, Emperor Shouhuang used the world to support the three halls of Deshou. When he traveled to the lakes and mountains, the food from the imperial kitchen was all delivered by the Hall Officials of the Ministry of Rites. Therefore, those who delivered cups and dishes in front of the imperial banquet were all Hall Officials. If someone mistakenly thought they were waiters, the store owner would quickly stop them and say, "No, they are Hall Officials." Therefore, it has become a common practice to this day. No one does not respect the waiters as Hall Officials. The caskets and mats used by the people of Hangzhou for sweeping graves were also made according to palace regulations for carrying wine when traveling. There is also this item in Dream of the Red Chamber. Its shape is like an examination basket, made of wood, slightly like a sacrificial vessel. Every four drawers are stacked together to form a hip flask. Each drawer is divided into six compartments, which can hold twenty-four dishes. Next to it are placed wine vessels, chopsticks, and mats. When drinking on the ground, the mats are spread out. They are about two feet square and can be folded in half. There is leather lining on the outside, and two ears can be lifted. During the Qing Dynasty, the incense sedan chairs of the government officials were all hung with mats, and the senior officials had boxes carried by two men behind the sedan chair. Some say it is a crime clothes box to serve the emperor. Once he is angered, he will be stripped of his position, so he must prepare crime clothes. All ranks below his current rank are prepared, so the great officials of the first and second ranks have more than nine pieces of clothing prepared.

West Lake water shield, some say it comes from Xiaoshan Xiang Lake, but it is not known that the water shield of Xiang Lake actually came from West Lake. The Qiantang County Records of the Wanli period say that the water shield grows in West Lake and is harvested in late spring and early summer. There are ice bells attached under the leaves. It used to be said that it was produced in Xiang Lake, but it is not known that the people of Xiang Lake came here to take it. The first shoots are tender and have no leaves, called Pheasant Tail Water Shield, also known as Horseshoe Water Shield. When the leaves are stretched out, they are called Silk Water Shield. In autumn, no one picks them. Li Liufang's Water Shield Soup Song says that West Lake water shield is sold in Xiaoshan for thousands of burdens, and Xiang Lake is full of them. He also made West Lake Lying Tour Album. In the postscript of picking water shield at Three Pools, he praised the beauty of the water shield, but he did not know that there is no water shield in Xiang Lake, and all of them are picked from West Lake. It is also said that the water shield is not good if it is not soaked in Xiang Lake water. It is not known that the water shield must be soaked overnight when it is first picked to make it more fertile. All spring water and lake water are acceptable and do not have to be Xiang Lake. The boat in the picture is full of water shield sellers from Xiaoshan. There are many poems about water shield, but the most appropriate one is Zhang Suichen's use of the three words "smooth flow spoon", which is indeed only suitable for water shield soup. Those who do not know the cooking method usually only leave the leaves and no longer have the so-called ice bells. Ice bells are the shape of the starch in the stem, which naturally condenses and is attached to the leaves, transparent like dewdrops, smooth and non-sticky. But if you wash it with cold water, it will still exist. If you boil it, it will dissolve and disappear without any meaning, equal to pea seedlings.

Yarn and Cotton Market Turns Downward

The yarn market weakened. Sales of spot yarn were still good. The Guangdong merchants actively purchased, so 16-count and 20-count yarns sold well. Japan also bought 200 bales of 16-count Ren Zhong yarn at a price of 166 taels without tax. However, the business of 10-count coarse yarn was sluggish. There were about 20,000 bales of yarn in the yarn warehouse, so the sellers were bold. Although there were 20,000 to 30,000 bales of sales in the north, the cloth market failed to be stimulated due to the lack of sales of coarse yarn. Furthermore, there was a rumor that a major merchant would sell the standard yarn for this month at 63 taels. If it falls to around 60 taels, they will purchase it. Therefore, market sentiment softened, and the sellers' pressure increased. The overseas yarn situation was still flat. The market atmosphere fell further in the afternoon due to the decline in gold prices. However, the bottom stock of fine yarn was reduced, and export transactions have been continuous recently.

Standard Yarn Falls by One Tael. Due to the decline in foreign cotton prices, the market sentiment was weak in the morning. There was a lack of buyers in the market, and prices fell by 0.03-0.08. In the afternoon, the market situation worsened as the gold price closed lower, and prices fell by another 0.04-0.08 for each month. The transaction volume was 28,150 bales. The sellers were Gongtai (1,200 bales), Gu Da (1,000 bales), Changfeng (800 bales), and Yichang (700 bales). The buyers were Yiyu (2,500 bales), Yicheng (900 bales), Shenxin (900 bales), Gengfeng (900 bales), and Dafu (700 bales). The closing prices are recorded below:

Cotton Market: Small Investors Selling Short

The cotton market is trending downward due to the decline in American cotton prices, the weak yarn market, and the lack of actual sales. Market sentiment has softened. However, Hankou cotton prices are firm due to a shortage of goods, so there is still some optimism. However, most small investors are inclined to sell short.

Hankou Standard Falls by 0.03. The morning opening price for Hankou standard cotton fell by 0.02-0.03 due to unfavorable foreign cotton prices. The afternoon opening price was weak due to the declining gold price. The closing price rebounded, with the distant months falling by 0.01. The total transaction volume for the day was 39,400 dan. US Cotton Frequently Reaches New Lows Last Week

Private Estimates of Cotton Fields Reduced by About 10.1%

New York, May 5th Report on the Cotton Market Conditions of the Past Week: The Cotton Market in the past week was hindered by the changes in the securities market. At the beginning of the week, it hit a new low for the season, mainly due to long liquidation by brokers on Wall Street and in Europe. However, the securities market quickly rebounded, and banks and brokers also reduced the required margin, while the purchase of government bonds exceeded expectations. All of this helped to restore confidence. The weather was generally good, but some areas still needed rain. According to five private estimates, cotton fields were reduced by about 10.1%. Spot demand in the South showed a slight increase, and foreign yarn mills had more confidence in the current market prices, so there were increasing rumors of increased exports. The cotton market was quiet, and buyers were skeptical. The weekend statistics are attached below (unit: thousands of bales):

Silk and Tea: Wuxi Xinxinzhou Releases Prices and Competes to Collect Superior Cocoons

Improved Variety High-Quality Goods Have Opened at 62-3 Yuan

In Wuxi, more than a hundred cocoon firms in various markets and villages uniformly opened the scale yesterday. This year, the cocoon production in Xiyi was surprisingly poor. Only the late [unclear] cocoons had a slightly better harvest, but the total was less than one-third of the previous year. The arrival of goods in the market was not prosperous. Although various cocoon merchants had a proposal to limit the cocoon price, the number of receipts was so small that farmers insisted on selling high-quality cocoons at high prices, and they had to release prices and compete for collection. In the cocoons firms such as Baochang in Qianzhou, Beixinqiao, Shichuang, and Beiqifang, the price for competing to collect improved high-quality cocoons has been raised to 62-3 yuan. The price of high-quality goods in other markets and villages has also risen to 56-7 yuan.

Social News

German Pocket Battleship Surprises Major Naval Powers

Mechanical Materials All Use Light Metals to Save 1,700 Tons of Ship Weight——Breaking the Eastern Restraint of the Versailles Treaty——

Berlin News: The Washington Conference stipulates that the tonnage of battleships is limited to a maximum of 35,000 tons, and the Versailles Treaty further stipulates that Germany may not manufacture battleships of more than 11,000 tons. Under this restriction, the German Navy Department has spent many years researching and testing a new 10,000-ton pocket battleship. Its clever shipbuilding technology has alarmed the major powers. The machinery installed in the ship is made of light metal, which can save 1,700 tons of ship weight. There are unexpected installations in the armament and armor. There are six 16-inch cannons and eight 5-inch cannons. The new cannons of the aircraft have four turrets for launching torpedoes. Its combat power is unmatched among the battleships of major powers. The manufacturing cost is 40 million marks, and the endurance of the town's voyage is the most durable. It only needs to replenish fuel once from Germany to China.

Development of Aviation Industry in Portugal

Land, Sea, and Commercial Talents All Have Construction

Lisbon News: Portugal's aviation industry has made considerable progress in recent years. According to the latest statistics, the Portuguese Army Aviation Bureau currently has 50 pilots and 60 aircraft hangars. There are 20 temporary landing grounds set up throughout the country. It is now planned to build airports in Lisbon and Vao Poto. The Naval Aviation Bureau has 15 pilots and 25 seaplanes. There are currently 4 commercial pilots. The commercial flight business is now fully managed by the Portuguese Aviation Company and will soon begin flying.
